***avenger.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:avenger.html>avenger</a> (95625)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Latn mention" lang="en">avenge</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:dictatoriaal.html>-er</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:avenger.html>avenger</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:avengers.html>avengers</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>One who avenges or vindicates
<dl><dd><i>an <b><a href = vnd.unilang:avenger.html>avenger</a></b> of blood</i></dd></dl></li>
<li>One who <a href = vnd.unilang:takes.html>takes</a> vengeance.</li></ol>

***averechts.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:averechts.html>averechts</a> (42593)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:averechts.html>averechts</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">backwards, in the wrong direction</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">averecht</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">upside down, backwards, wrong</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">ave</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:recht.html>recht</a></i>, equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:af.html>af</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:rechts.html>rechts</a></i>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:averechts.html>averechts</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:averechts.html>averechtser</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:meest.html>meest</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:averechts.html>averechts</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">averechtst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>opposite, backwards, contrary
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:wat.html>Wat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nu.html>nu</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:doet.html>doet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:werkt.html>werkt</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:averechts.html>averechts</a></b>.</i>
<dl><dd>What you're doing now <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> the <b>opposite</b> effect of what you're trying to achieve.</dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ol>

***avond.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:avond.html>avond</a> (510)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">âvont</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">āvont</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*ēbanþs</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:avond.html>avond</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:avonden.html>avonden</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:avondje.html>avondje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>evening, night</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>Just like German <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Abend</i>, Dutch <i><a href = vnd.unilang:avond.html>avond</a></i> includes the <a href = vnd.unilang:hours.html>hours</a> until midnight. So while one says in English: <i><a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>We</a>'re having a <a href = vnd.unilang:beer.html>beer</a> tonight!</i>, one would say in Dutch: <i><a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>We</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:drinken.html>drinken</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vanavond.html>vanavond</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:biertje.html>biertje</a>!</i>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>

***avondmaal.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:avondmaal.html>avondmaal</a> (13222)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">avontmael</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:avond.html>avond</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">evening</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:maal.html>maal</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">meal</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:avondmaal.html>avondmaal</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:avondmaal.html>avondmalen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:avondmaal.html>avondmaaltje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>dinner, supper, the evening meal
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>Het</a></i> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:avondmaal.html>avondmaal</a></b> <i><a href = vnd.unilang:staat.html>staat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:klaar.html>klaar</a>.</i>
<dl><dd><i>Dinner <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> ready.</i></dd></dl></dd>
<dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>Het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:laatste.html>Laatste</a></i> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:avondmaal.html>Avondmaal</a></b> <i><a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:beroemd.html>beroemd</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:schilderij.html>schilderij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> Leonardo da Vinci.</i>
<dl><dd><i>The Last Supper <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> a famous painting by Leonardo da Vinci.</i></dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>This word tends to be used only to refer to "regular" dinners <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> at home, not to dinner parties or meals eaten elsewhere, where <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:diner.html>diner</a></i> or <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:avondeten.html>avondeten</a></i> are much more often used.
</p>

***avondster.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:avondster.html>avondster</a> (85058)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">âvontsterre</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:avond.html>avond</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ster.html>ster</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:avondster.html>avondster</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:avondster.html>avondsterren</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:avondster.html>avondsterretje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">astronomy</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Evening star; the planet Venus as seen in the western sky in the evening.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">astronomy</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Evening star; any star seen in the evening, <i>especially</i> the planets Mercury and Jupiter.</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">aventure</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">aventure</i>. The <i><a href = vnd.unilang:o.html>o</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> due to influence from <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:avond.html>avond</a></i>, which <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> also affected the pronunciation.

***avontuurlijk.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:avontuurlijk.html>avontuurlijk</a> (17897)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">aventuerlijc</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">avontuerlijc</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">avonturlic</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:avontuur.html>avontuur</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">adventure</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-lijk</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">-ly</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:avontuurlijk.html>avontuurlijk</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:avontuurlijk.html>avontuurlijker</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">avontuurlijkst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>Like an adventure, dangerous, eventful, exciting
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:wat.html>Wat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:avontuurlijk.html>avontuurlijke</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:reis.html>reis</a>! <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>Zijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:verhaal.html>verhaal</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:boeiend.html>boeiender</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dan.html>dan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:tv.html>Tv</a>.</i>
<dl><dd><i>What an exciting journey! His story <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> more fascinating then <a href = vnd.unilang:tv.html>Tv</a>.</i></dd></dl></dd></dl></li>
<li>Daring, adventurous, accepting <a href = vnd.unilang:risks.html>risks</a></li></ol>

***aye.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:aye.html>aye</a> (7010)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href = vnd.unilang:aye.html>aye</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">ai</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">aȝȝ</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Norse" class="extiw" title="w:Old Norse">Old <a href = vnd.unilang:norse.html>Norse</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="non"><a href = vnd.unilang:ei.html>ei</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="non">ey</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*aiwa</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*aiwō</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">ever, always</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (compare <span class="etyl"><a <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">ā</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">ō</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:ie.html>ie</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a></i>), from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*aiwaz</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">age; law</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">ǣ(w)</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">law</span><span title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">ieu</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:eeuw.html>eeuw</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">century</span><span class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*h₂eyu-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">long time</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren Doublet of <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">aevum</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:aye.html>aye</a></strong> (<i>not comparable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">archaic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> ever, always
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1610–1611</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/William_Shakespeare" class="extiw" title="w:William Shakespeare">William Shakespeare</a>,  “<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Tempest" class="extiw" title="w:The Tempest">The Tempest</a>”, in  <cite><a href = vnd.unilang:mr.html>Mr</a>. William Shakespeares Comedies, <a href = vnd.unilang:histories.html>Histories</a>, amp; <a href = vnd.unilang:tragedies.html>Tragedies</a>: Published <a href = vnd.unilang:according.html>According</a> to the True Originall <a href = vnd.unilang:copies.html>Copies</a></cite> (<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/First_Folio" class="extiw" title="w:First Folio">First Folio</a>), London |  Printed by <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/William_Jaggard" class="extiw" title="w:William Jaggard">Isaac Iaggard</a>, and <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Edward_Blount" class="extiw" title="w:Edward Blount">Ed[ward] Blount</a>, published 1623, <small><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/OCLC" class="extiw" title="w:OCLC">OCLC</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://worldcat.org/oclc/606515358">606515358</a></small>, [Act IV, scene i]:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en"><span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span>Do that good miſcheefe, which may make this Iſland / Thine owne for euer, and I thy <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Caliban" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Caliban">Caliban</a></i>, / For <b><a href = vnd.unilang:aye.html>aye</a></b> thy foot-licker.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><b>1834</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Samuel_Taylor_Coleridge" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Samuel Taylor Coleridge">Samuel <a href = vnd.unilang:taylor.html>Taylor</a> Coleridge</a>, "The Rime of the Ancient Mariner":
<dl><dd>The ship drove fast, loud roared the blast, / And southward <b><a href = vnd.unilang:aye.html>aye</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> fled.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1863</b>, Translation by <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Catherine_Winkworth" class="extiw" title="w:Catherine Winkworth"><a href = vnd.unilang:catherine.html>Catherine</a> Winkworth</a>:
<dl><dd>Let the <a href = vnd.unilang:amen.html>Amen</a> sound from His people again; Gladly for <b><a href = vnd.unilang:aye.html>aye</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> adore Him. (<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Praise_to_the_Lord,_the_Almighty" class="extiw" title="w:Praise to the Lord, the Almighty">Praise to the Lord, the Almighty</a>)</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Probably from use of <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:aye.html>aye</a></i> as expression of agreement or affirmation, or from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">a ye</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:oh.html>oh</a> yes</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, or synthesis of both. More at <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:oh.html>oh</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">yea</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Interjection">Interjection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:aye.html>aye</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>yes; yea; a word expressing assent, or an affirmative answer to a question.</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li>It <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> much used in <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Scottish_English" class="extiw" title="w:Scottish English">Scotland</a>, the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Northern_English" class="extiw" title="w:Northern English">north</a> and <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language_in_EnglandMidlands" class="extiw" title="w:English language in England">Midlands</a> of England, the northern <a href = vnd.unilang:counties.html>counties</a> of <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hiberno_English" class="extiw" title="w:Hiberno English">Ireland</a>, North Wales, as well as in Australia and New Zealand (where it may follow rather than precede a statement). Also notably seen in <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">viva voce</i> voting in legislative <a href = vnd.unilang:bodies.html>bodies</a>, etc., or in nautical contexts.</li></ul>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">yes</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">yea</span></li></ul>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:aye.html>aye</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">ayes</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>An affirmative vote; one who votes in the affirmative.
<dl><dd><i>"To call for the <b>ayes</b> and nays;" "The <b>ayes</b> have it."</i></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms_2">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">yes</span></li></ul>
</body>

***baa.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:baa.html>baa</a> (95600)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">bäh</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">mäh</i>; an imitative word.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:baa.html>baa</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:baas.html>baas</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">onomatopoeia</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The characteristic cry or bleating of a sheep.</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">bleat</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">bleating</span></li></ul>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Interjection">Interjection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:baa.html>baa</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">onomatopoeia</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="use-with-mention">The characteristic cry of a sheep.</span></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:baa.html>baa</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:baas.html>baas</a></b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">baaing</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">baaed</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>To make the characteristic cry of a sheep.
<ul><li><b>1590-1593</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Philip_Sidney" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Philip Sidney">Philip <a href = vnd.unilang:sidney.html>Sidney</a></a>, <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Countess_of_Pembroke%27s_Arcadia" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:The Countess of Pembroke | s Arcadia">The Countess of Pembroke's <a href = vnd.unilang:arcadia.html>Arcadia</a></a></i>
<dl><dd>He treble <b><a href = vnd.unilang:baas.html>baas</a></b> for help, but none can get.</dd></dl></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1902</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Barbara_Baynton" class="extiw" title="w:Barbara Baynton">Barbara Baynton</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:sally.html>Sally</a> Krimmer; Alan <a href = vnd.unilang:lawson.html>Lawson</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:editors.html>editors</a>, <cite>Bush Studies</cite> (<a href = vnd.unilang:portable.html>Portable</a> Australian Authors: Barbara Baynton), St Lucia |  University of Queensland Press, published 1980, page 44:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">The lamb bunted several irresponsive <a href = vnd.unilang:objects.html>objects</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:halal.html>-</a> never its dam's udder <a href = vnd.unilang:halal.html>-</a> <b>baaing</b> listlessly.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Arabic" class="extiw" title="w:Arabic">Arabic</a></span></span> <i class="Arab mention" lang="ar">بَاء</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ar-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bāʾ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

</p>
<ol><li>The letter <span class="Arab" lang="und">ب</span> |  in the Arabic script.</li></ol>

<p>Directly or ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm">baie</i>. <span class="maintenance-line"><i>This etymology <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> incomplete. ***baan.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:baan.html>baan</a> (566)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">bāne</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*bana</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*banō</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:baan.html>baan</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:banen.html>banen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:baantje.html>baantje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>a road, way, path
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zit.html>zit</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:al.html>al</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:acht.html>acht</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:uur.html>uur</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:baan.html>baan</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">I've <a href = vnd.unilang:sat.html>sat</a> on the <b>road</b> for eight <a href = vnd.unilang:hours.html>hours</a> already.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>a track, lane</li>
<li>a job, professional occupation
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:heb.html>heb</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nieuwe.html>nieuwe</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:baan.html>baan</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">I've got a new <b>job</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">sports<span class="ib-comma">,</span> ball games</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> court, field <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">place for playing sports or games, in particular non-team ball games</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:baan.html>baan</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="use-with-mention">first-person singular present indicative of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:banen.html>banen</a></i></span></li>
<li><span class="use-with-mention">  imperative of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:banen.html>banen</a></i></span></li></ol>

***baar.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:baar.html>baar</a> (25466)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_2">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">bâre</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt"><a href = vnd.unilang:bier.html>bier</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-West_Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-West Germanic language">Proto-West Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*bērō</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*bērō</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*bʰer-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to carry, bear</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Saterland_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Saterland Frisian language">Saterland Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="stq">Beere</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">stretcher, <a href = vnd.unilang:bier.html>bier</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:bier.html>bier</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Bahre</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:bier.html>bier</a>, stretcher</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_6">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:baar.html>baar</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:baren.html>baren</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:baar.html>baartje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A <a href = vnd.unilang:bier.html>bier</a>, a stretcher, a litter; a device used to carry someone or something, especially wounded or dead people.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:draagbaar.html>draagbaar</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>A <a href = vnd.unilang:bed.html>bed</a> on which a dead person <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> displayed before he <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> buried.
<ul><li><b>1922</b>, Albert Verwey, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:weg.html>weg</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:licht.html>licht</a></i>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.dbnl.org/tekst/verw008wegv01_01/verw008wegv01_01_0028.htm"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> Gerichte <a href = vnd.unilang:wil.html>Wil</a></a>
<dl><dd><a href = vnd.unilang:wanneer.html>Wanneer</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:stierf.html>stierf</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zij.html>zij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:mij.html>mij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:beminden.html>beminden</a> / <a href = vnd.unilang:rondom.html>Rondom</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:mijn.html>mijn</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:baar.html>baar</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:staan.html>staan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> d’<a href = vnd.unilang:andre.html>andre</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vraagt.html>vraagt</a>:
<dl><dd>When I died and those that <a href = vnd.unilang:loved.html>loved</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a> / stand around my <b>dead <a href = vnd.unilang:bed.html>bed</a></b> and one asks the other:</dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ul>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">bare</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro"><a href = vnd.unilang:barre.html>barre</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_7">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:baar.html>baar</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:baren.html>baren</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:baar.html>baartje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A <a href = vnd.unilang:bar.html>bar</a>, an ingot <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of gold or another metal</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A <a href = vnd.unilang:bar.html>bar</a>, a beam.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:boom.html>boom</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:staaf.html>staaf</a></span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:baard.html>baard</a> (4251)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">baert</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*bart</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-West_Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-West Germanic language">Proto-West Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*bard</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*bardaz</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*bʰardʰ-eh₂</i>.
</p>

***baas.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:baas.html>baas</a> (550)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">baes</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">master of a household, friend</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*baso</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">uncle, kinsman</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*baswô</i>. Cognates include <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Low German">Middle Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gml">bās</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">supervisor, <a href = vnd.unilang:foreman.html>foreman</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Frisian" class="extiw" title="w:Old Frisian">Old Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="ofs"><a href = vnd.unilang:bas.html>bas</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">master</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; possibly also <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">basa</i> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">"father's sister, cousin"; gt; German <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Base</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">aunt, cousin</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:baas.html>baas</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bazen.html>bazen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:baasje.html>baasje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bazin.html>bazin</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>boss, chief, superior</li>
<li>employer, manager</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Belgium" class="extiw" title="w:Belgium">Belgium</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> strong or tough guy</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">video games</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> boss</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> crack, master, expert at something</li>

***babbelen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:babbelen.html>babbelen</a> (8240)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:babbelen.html>babbelen</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*babbalon</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*babalōną</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:babbelen.html>babbelen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to chatter, to chit-chat, to talk casually</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">archaic<span class="ib-comma">,</span> dialectal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to nibble, to bite on something</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:baby.html>baby</a> (579)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:baby.html>baby</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:baby.html>baby</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:baby.html>baby</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-foon</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">-phone</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:babysit.html>babysit</a> (30074)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Back-formation from <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:babysitter.html>babysitter</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:babysit.html>babysit</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">babysits</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">babysitting</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">babysat</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>To watch or tend someone else's child for a period of time, often for money.
<dl><dd><i>My daughter <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <b>babysitting</b> for the <a href = vnd.unilang:morgans.html>Morgans</a> at number ten, who are going out on a date night.</i></dd>
<dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>We</a> need someone to <b><a href = vnd.unilang:babysit.html>babysit</a></b> our children while <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> go to the <a href = vnd.unilang:theater.html>theater</a>.</i></dd></dl>
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2012</b> May 27,  Nathan Rabin,  “TV: Review: THE SIMPSONS (CLASSIC): “New Kid On The Block” (season 4, episode 8; originally aired 11/12/1992)”, in  <cite>The Onion AV Club</cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="https://www.avclub.com/articles/new-kid-on-the-block,75341/">[1]</a></sup>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Bart eventually <a href = vnd.unilang:gets.html>gets</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:laura.html>Laura</a> to <b><a href = vnd.unilang:babysit.html>babysit</a></b> while <a href = vnd.unilang:homer.html>Homer</a> and <a href = vnd.unilang:marge.html>Marge</a> eat at the Sea <a href = vnd.unilang:captain.html>Captain</a>’s all-you-can-eat seafood joint, The Frying <a href = vnd.unilang:dutchman.html>Dutchman</a>.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> informal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To watch or attend anything or anyone unnecessarily closely; to have to help or coax too much.
<dl><dd><i>He left <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a> to <b><a href = vnd.unilang:babysit.html>babysit</a></b> the new guy while he got some work done.</i></dd></dl>

***babysitter.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:babysitter.html>babysitter</a> (9010)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:baby.html>baby</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">sitter</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:babysitter.html>babysitter</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:babysitters.html>babysitters</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A person who cares for one or more <a href = vnd.unilang:babies.html>babies</a> or children for a short period of time in place of their legal <a href = vnd.unilang:guardians.html>guardians</a>.
<dl><dd><i>My neighbor <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> sometimes a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:babysitter.html>babysitter</a></b> for other moms' children.</i></dd></dl></li></ol>

***baccarat.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:baccarat.html>baccarat</a> (55085)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr"><a href = vnd.unilang:baccarat.html>baccarat</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">baccara</i> <span class="defdate">[19th c.]</span>, likely named after the French town <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Baccarat" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Baccarat"><a href = vnd.unilang:baccarat.html>Baccarat</a></a> (noted for glassmaking) in Grand Est, of ultimately unclear and debated origin <span class="defdate">[1291?]</span>. If by some <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Vulgar_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Vulgar Latin">Vulgar Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">*Bacchara</i>, the town <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> possibly named from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">Bacchi</i> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href = vnd.unilang:ara.html>ara</a></i> ("altar of Bacchus"; the original pagan reference of the name <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:forgotten.html>forgotten</a>), name of an ancient Roman <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">castellum</i>, of which there <a href = vnd.unilang:remains.html>remains</a> a relic called the "Tower of Bacha" on the heights of Deneuvre, from whence <a href = vnd.unilang:baccarat.html>Baccarat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> an ancient suburb. Other <a href = vnd.unilang:hypotheses.html>hypotheses</a> have also <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> suggested, including descent from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Celtic_languages" class="extiw" title="w:Celtic languages">Celtic</a></span>.
</p><p>Probably linked to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proven%C3%A7al_dialect" class="extiw" title="w:Provençal dialect">Provençal</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="oc">baccara</i>, although if the town etymology <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> correct, this may present some geographic difficulty.
</p>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/94/Au_bac.jpg/220px-Au_bac.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="266" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/94/Au_bac.jpg/330px-Au_bac.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/94/Au_bac.jpg/440px-Au_bac.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1213" data-file-height="1468" />  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"></div>A game of <b><a href = vnd.unilang:baccarat.html>baccarat</a></b>, illustrated from 1897 by <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Albert_Guillaume" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Albert Guillaume">Albert Guillaume</a>.</div></div></div>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:baccarat.html>baccarat</a></strong> (<i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">card games</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A card game resembling <a href = vnd.unilang:chemin.html>chemin</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> fer with many forms <a href = vnd.unilang:halal.html>-</a> usually entailing the player(s) betting against two or three hands <a href = vnd.unilang:dealt.html>dealt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:halal.html>-</a> also bearing some similarities to blackjack.</li></ol>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>By far, the most common style played <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:punto.html>punto</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:banco.html>banco</a></i>, where the closest total value to 9 between a pair of cards by "Player" or "Banker" wins.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:baccarat.html>baccarat</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic"><a href = vnd.unilang:o.html>o</a></span> <sup id="cite_ref-4" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-4"> | 4 | </a></sup>
</p>
<ol><li><span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(<a href = vnd.unilang:spel.html>spel</a>)</span> gokspel <a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kaarten.html>kaarten</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:waarbij.html>waarbij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:drie.html>drie</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:tot.html>tot</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:elf.html>elf</a>) <a href = vnd.unilang:deelnemers.html>deelnemers</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:spelen.html>spelen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:tegen.html>tegen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> bankhouder (<a href = vnd.unilang:baccarat.html>baccarat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:banque.html>banque</a>) of <a href = vnd.unilang:onder.html>onder</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:elkaar.html>elkaar</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:baccarat.html>baccarat</a> chemin-de-fer) <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:twee.html>twee</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kaarten.html>kaarten</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:eventueel.html>eventueel</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:derde.html>derde</a>, aanvullende <a href = vnd.unilang:kaart.html>kaart</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:negen.html>negen</a> of <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dichtst.html>dichtst</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:daarbij.html>daarbij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:uit.html>uit</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:moeten.html>moeten</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:komen.html>komen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:om.html>om</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:inzet.html>inzet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:winnen.html>winnen</a></li>
<li><a href = vnd.unilang:fijn.html>fijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:glaswerk.html>glaswerk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ruitjes.html>ruitjes</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:oorspronkelijk.html>oorspronkelijk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:afkomstig.html>afkomstig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:uit.html>uit</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:franse.html>Franse</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:stad.html>stad</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:baccarat.html>Baccarat</a> <sup id="cite_ref-5" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-5"> | 5 | </a></sup></li></ol>

***backgammon.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:backgammon.html>backgammon</a> (32057)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Probably from <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">back</i> + <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href = vnd.unilang:gamen.html>gamen</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang"><a href = vnd.unilang:gamen.html>gamen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">amusement, game</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:152px;"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/30/Backgammon_lg.jpg/150px-Backgammon_lg.jpg" decoding="async" width="150" height="100" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/30/Backgammon_lg.jpg/225px-Backgammon_lg.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/30/Backgammon_lg.jpg/300px-Backgammon_lg.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1500" data-file-height="1000" />  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"></div>A <a href = vnd.unilang:backgammon.html>backgammon</a> board shown in starting position.</div></div></div>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:backgammon.html>backgammon</a></strong> (<i>countable and uncountable</i>, <i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">backgammons</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A board game for two players in which each <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> 15 stones which move between 24 triangular points <a href = vnd.unilang:according.html>according</a> to the roll of a pair of dice; the object <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> to move all of one's pieces around, and bear them off the board.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:backgammon.html>backgammon</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A victory in the game when the <a href = vnd.unilang:loser.html>loser</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> not borne off a stone, and still <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> one or more stones in the winner's inner home row or on the <a href = vnd.unilang:bar.html>bar</a>.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">gammon</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:backgammon.html>backgammon</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">backgammons</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">backgammoning</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">backgammoned</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>To win at a <a href = vnd.unilang:backgammon.html>backgammon</a> game with the opponent having one or more pieces in the winner’s inner home row or on the <a href = vnd.unilang:bar.html>bar</a>.</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:backgammon.html>backgammon</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic"><a href = vnd.unilang:o.html>o</a></span>
</p>
<ol><li><span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(<a href = vnd.unilang:spel.html>spel</a>)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> triktrak <a href = vnd.unilang:afgeleid.html>afgeleid</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bordspel.html>bordspel</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:voor.html>voor</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:twee.html>twee</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:personen.html>personen</a></li></ol>
<p><br />
</p>
</body>

***backhand.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:backhand.html>backhand</a> (32803)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">back</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">hand</i>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:backhand.html>backhand</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">backhands</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">tennis</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> a stroke made across the chest from the off-hand side to the racquet hand side; a stroke during which the back of the hand <a href = vnd.unilang:faces.html>faces</a> the shot.</li>
<li>Handwriting that leans to the left</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">Ultimate <a href = vnd.unilang:frisbee.html>Frisbee</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> the standard throw; a throw during which the disc begins on the off-hand side and travels across the chest to be released from the opposite side.</li>
<li>The reverse side of the human hand.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">surfing</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> the hand towards the back of the board.</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:backhand.html>backhand</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">backhands</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">backhanding</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">backhanded</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to execute a <a href = vnd.unilang:backhand.html>backhand</a> stroke or throw</li>
<li>to <a href = vnd.unilang:slap.html>slap</a> with the back of one's hand</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:backhand.html>backhand</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en comparative-form-of" lang="en">more <a href = vnd.unilang:backhand.html>backhand</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en superlative-form-of" lang="en">most <a href = vnd.unilang:backhand.html>backhand</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">handwriting</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Of any left slanting handwriting</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">of strokes or throws</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> In the <a href = vnd.unilang:backhand.html>backhand</a> style</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">ice hockey</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Of a play that uses the back side of the hockey stick
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">He scored on a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:backhand.html>backhand</a></b> shot.</i></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:backhand.html>backhand</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">v</span>/(<span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">m</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(sport)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:achterwaartse.html>achterwaartse</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:slag.html>slag</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a> bijv. <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:tennisracket.html>tennisracket</a>
